There are two bathrooms in the room, and the detergents are L'Occitane.
The bathroom brand is Kohler. But it is not an automatic toilet.
Both doors can use room cards, front and back yards, the front yard is smaller, and the back yard can accommodate at least eight people for barbecue. You can overlook the scenery behind, with pomegranate trees and bamboos, and the scenery is beautiful.
The room design is also reasonable, the bedroom is high, and the view is very comfortable.
The wall painting is a palace design of textile fabrics, part of which is embroidered, which is a**ospheric and upscale.
The sound system is Harman Kardon, the sound quality is quite good, and it can be regarded as a top enjoyment.
The service is also very good, butler-style service.
Although there is a certain distance from the lobby to the room, it is not far. There is a shuttle bus at the hotel front desk, which can pick up guests at any time.
The hotel maintenance costs are very high. Although the gym and swimming pool are not open, many details need to be improved, but it is much better than expected and can be regarded as the top luxury hotel.
Songpin is located in the suburbs, which is also the problem of cheap housing prices. But it is really suitable for people like me who like quietness. It is great. It is suitable for a quiet vacation without too many people coming and going.
Basically, I will stay here when I come to Jinan in the future.
